name:A‚Äçn‚Äçt‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçi‚Äça
info:Stayed in November 2021
info:Family
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted November 28, 2021
msg:The location is beautiful, the staff was super nice. It's placed on an island, the hotel provides electric cars to drive the guests from the parking lot over a wooden bridge to the resort. There is a lot to do and just the walk around the resort itself is worth the time with awesome views. The breakfast was very rich of choices, the coffee was not the best, may be caused by the taste of the tap water at the hotel. There is a coffee shop, small travel agency and a small workshop place for kids directly in the lobby. There's another coffee shop outside with a beautiful view. The hotel set up swings, benches, tables on different places to enjoy all the views. 
We had Lake-view Twin room. The view was fantastic. We liked the room, there were 4 kinds of tea, instant coffee and latte and water for refreshing. The room was clean and good equipped. Our only complain was that the walls in the shower weren't cleaned properly, after we asked to clean them it was visible how high could the cleaning lady reach. The water in the swimming pool was nicely warm, the changing rooms weren't heated though. However, I think the indoor swimming pool area needs some reconstruction (clean the walls of the pool from mildew for instance). All in all we are definitely coming back soon with other family members!

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom - Lake-View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:Self-driving for three days and two nights from Hangzhou.

Navigation directly locates Wenxin Island Dielai Hotel, the car is parked in the exclusive parking lot, and the shuttle bus will directly send people and luggage to the hotel (the wooden floating bridge takes about three or two minutes, the master said that it is usually at 10 pm at the latest), and the front desk will scan the code when leaving the hotel to waive parking fees.

There are two hotels on the island. Dielai is larger in overall scale than Zhiya, and it was established a few years earlier than Zhiya, so the electrical appliances and bathroom equipment are older. In addition, the hotel location, room layout, window scenery, supporting facilities, services, travel convenience and other aspects are perfect.

Fortunately, the front desk helped to upgrade the room type and live on the 4th floor of the villa area. Most of the room types are on the first and second floors (the hotel lobby is on the second floor), and the room types on the third and fourth floors belong to the villa area. Indoor swimming pool, KTV, gym, billiard room, table tennis, massage, etc. are on the first floor. The gym is relatively small at night and closes at 10 o'clock. You can go at any time in the morning.

It is convenient to travel. Take the car out of the island and turn right to the Qiandao Lake Bridge. After crossing the bridge, turn right for three minutes to reach the Tianyu Mountain Scenic Area. Then drive for more than ten minutes to the commercial area and the Central Lake Scenic Area Visitor Center.

This time the schedule was not too full. Most of the time was spent in the hotel and on the island. It felt very comfortable and relaxed. Overall, it was more pleasant than expected.

There are a lot of places to eat within a few kilometers of the hotel, and it's not far from the Fish Street, where most locals go.

name:H‚Äça‚Äçi‚Äçb‚Äçu‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçk‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçi‚Äçq‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Family
info:27 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted April 11, 2023
msg:General situation: Dielai is located on the east side of Wenxin Island, which is adjacent to the Qiandao Lake Bridge to the west. The hotel is large in scale and runs north-south. The main building has five floors, the lobby has been upgraded on the second floor, and the villa area is located on the south side of the main building on the 1st to 3rd floors. To check in, you need to get off the elevator on the 3rd floor and take the walkway. The ground on the 3rd floor looks like A detached villa, in fact, the bottom two floors are connected to the main building, and the large corridor looks like a maze. The wooden houses are not connected to the main building and villas, the first four of which are being upgraded and constructed, and only the southernmost wooden house b5 can be lived in.
Environment: Compared with the buildings in Greentown and the Intercontinental, Dielai is really on the island in the middle of the lake. The environment is quiet, and the guest rooms face east, west, and south. It is good to watch the sunset or the scenery during the day and night, and there are not many people fishing on the trestle bridge. Less, but because the parking lot is far away from the island, it is inconvenient to enter and exit the hotel.
Facilities and sanitation: To be honest, all the points mentioned in the bad reviews have been met. Cockroaches slipped past the door of the booked wooden house. The front desk said that there are more mosquitoes near the water, which I can understand, but the appearance of cockroaches must indicate that there are food residues that have not been cleaned, and some areas of the carpet and tabletop are also stained. After reporting to the front desk, it was changed to a villa with twin beds. The room type was upgraded but the facilities were still old. The faucet handle fell off and the cabinet doors were often broken. The hardware situation of the hotel is worrying, and the sanitation situation is not optimistic.
Service: Generally speaking, the service level is reflected. From the doorman in the parking lot to welcome guests, the pick-up and drop-off of the battery car, the quality of food and beverages, and the timely handling of room problems after reporting them to the front desk, we can see the service level of Dielai as an old-fashioned luxury hotel. The standard is still high.
Postscript: As a subsidiary of Zhejiang Tourism Inves**ent Group, Dielai's image as a state-owned enterprise is the basis for tourists' trust. This can be seen from the proud look of the doorman when introducing the hotel. However, the problem of aging and poor sanitation of old hotel facilities is wearing down the patience of tourists. State-owned enterprises should have the responsibility of state-owned enterprises, instead of simply replying sorry to the negative reviews of tourists, and not relying on casually upgrading the room type to gain favor. The driver of the battery car at night not only has to pick up and drop off passengers, but also takes passengers up and down multiple floors to change rooms and carry luggage. I can understand her hard work, but I can't understand the problems that other passengers have found on the intercom. ! ! Which one is the hotel logo? Radisson, Zhejiang Travel Inves**ent and Dielai are dotted in the lobby and in the rooms without unity.
ps: Dielai is currently the most suitable for people on vacation and leisure (don‚Äôt take a boat to jump to the island to play attractions, just lie in the house in a daze), the room type is not recommended to live in a wooden house, the first four buildings are under construction, and the only one has a higher room density , the sound insulation is poor and the viewing effect is average, it is acceptable to live in villas and ordinary rooms in the main building. If you want to see the sunrise or lake view, choose a1/3/7/8. The rest of the villas basically face northwest, and there are other small islands blocking the view of the central lake area.

In the evening, I ordered a big fish head soup, the ceiling in the fish soup! The hotel package includes two cups of milk tea with ice every day, which is good üëç, and you can enjoy coffee and tea in the lobby bar. The indoor pool is clean and not crowded. It is worth punching in the afternoon tea that takes 5 minutes to walk next to the hotel. It is recommended to go after 5:30 in summer. It is hotter in the open air without air conditioning. It can be cooler at night, and you can watch the sunset and the afterglow of the sunset, but it closes at 8:00 p.m. . The three-day and two-night vacation was very happy, and I even took a cruise. The hotel staff were also very enthusiastic, and the scenery on the island was superb!
